be (bii) v. waxaa loo isticmaalaa in ay falgargaare (subject) ku xirto weedh kale oo shay wax ka sheegaysa. Waxay kale oo wax ka sheegtaa wax jira ama dhacay iyo falal isku xiran (linking verbs) oo isku caawinaya qaabab kala duwan sida: 1 jiritaan; nolol. e.g. Ahmed-Gurey is no more. 2 wax dhici doona. e.g. The final game will be tomorrow. 3 wax jooga ama wali socda. e.g. They will be here until tonight. 4 wax dagsiimo leh. e.g. The house is on your right. Marka be ay u janjeersanayso dhinaca falka (verb), waxay ku xirmataa falgargaaraha (subject): 1 magac (noun) e.g. She is a teacher. 2 tilmaame (adjec tive) e.g. He is short. 3 magac u yaal (pronoun) e.g. Who is she? Marka be caawinayso ficilka. 1 a past participle. e.g. The camels are gone! 2 a present participle. e.g. I am going. 3 infinitive (fal wali socda) e.g. We have to finish the food later.
